27/05/22, 12:42â€¯pm - Beluga2.0: public class CommentAdapter extends RecyclerView.Adapter<CommentAdapter.ViewHolder> {

    private Context context;
    private List<CommentModel> commentModelList;

    public CommentAdapter(Context context, List<CommentModel> commentModelList) {
        this.context = context;
        this.commentModelList = commentModelList;
    }

    @NonNull
    @Override
    public ViewHolder onCreateViewHolder(@NonNull ViewGroup parent, int viewType) {
        View view = LayoutInflater.from(parent.getContext()).inflate(R.layout.comment_item,parent,false);
        return  new CommentAdapter.ViewHolder(view);
    }

    @Override
    public void onBindViewHolder(@NonNull ViewHolder holder, int position) {
        CommentModel model = commentModelList.get(position);

        holder.comment.setText(model.getComment());
        holder.userName.setText(model.getPublisherName());
        holder.date.setText(model.getCommentPostDate());

    }

    @Override
    public int getItemCount() {
        return commentModelList.size();
    }

    public class ViewHolder extends RecyclerView.ViewHolder {
        private CircleImageView userImage;
        private SocialTextView comment,userName;
        private TextView date;
        public ViewHolder(@NonNull View itemView) {
            super(itemView);
            userImage = itemView.findViewById(R.id.comment_user_image);
            userName = itemView.findViewById(R.id.comment_user_name);
            comment = itemView.findViewById(R.id.comment_text);
            date = itemView.findViewById(R.id.comment_date);
        }
    }
}
27/05/22, 12:42â€¯pm - Beluga2.0: Adapter code
27/05/22, 12:42â€¯pm - Beluga2.0: public class CommentModel {
    private String commentId;
    private String comment;
    private String commentImage;
    private String commentPostDate;
    private String commentPublisherId;
    private String publisherImage;
    private String publisherName;


    public CommentModel(String commentId, String comment, String commentImage, String commentPostDate, String commentPublisherId, String publisherImage, String publisherName) {
        this.commentId = commentId;
        this.comment = comment;
        this.commentImage = commentImage;
        this.commentPostDate = commentPostDate;
        this.commentPublisherId = commentPublisherId;
        this.publisherImage = publisherImage;
        this.publisherName = publisherName;
    }


    public String getCommentId() {
        return commentId;
    }

    public void setCommentId(String commentId) {
        this.commentId = commentId;
    }

    public String getComment() {
        return comment;
    }

    public void setComment(String comment) {
        this.comment = comment;
    }

    public String getCommentImage() {
        return commentImage;
    }

    public void setCommentImage(String commentImage) {
        this.commentImage = commentImage;
    }

    public String getCommentPostDate() {
        return commentPostDate;
    }

    public void setCommentPostDate(String commentPostDate) {
        this.commentPostDate = commentPostDate;
    }

    public String getCommentPublisherId() {
        return commentPublisherId;
    }

    public void setCommentPublisherId(String commentPublisherId) {
        this.commentPublisherId = commentPublisherId;
    }

    public String getPublisherImage() {
        return publisherImage;
    }

    public void setPublisherImage(String publisherImage) {
        this.publisherImage = publisherImage;
    }

    public String getPublisherName() {
        return publisherName;
    }

    public void setPublisherName(String publisherName) {
        this.publisherName = publisherName;
    }
}

import androidx.recyclerview.widget.LinearLayoutManager;

import android.os.Bundle;
import android.view.View;

import com.animeclubapp.animeclub.R;
import com.animeclubapp.animeclub.adapter.CommentAdapter;
import com.animeclubapp.animeclub.adapter.PostAdapter;
import com.animeclubapp.animeclub.model.CommentModel;
import com.animeclubapp.animeclub.model.PostModel;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;

public class CommentActivity extends AppCompatActivity {

    private RecyclerView recyclerView;
    private List<CommentModel> commentModelList;
    private CommentAdapter commentAdapter;

    @Override
    protected void onCreate(Bundle savedInstanceState) {
        super.onCreate(savedInstanceState);
        setContentView(R.layout.activity_comment);

        recyclerView = findViewById(R.id.comment_recycler_view);

        commentModelList = new ArrayList<>();

        commentModelList.add(new CommentModel("","Hello","","10 aug","","","Rohit"));
        commentModelList.add(new CommentModel("","Hii It is nice","","4 aug","","","mis sumire"));
        commentModelList.add(new CommentModel("","Man it is awesome","","4 aug","","","perman"));
        commentModelList.add(new CommentModel("","That is very cool","","6 jan","","","bobby"));
        commentModelList.add(new CommentModel("","Wow!!","","10 jun","","","payan"));
        commentModelList.add(new CommentModel("","that is excelent","","10 sep","","","doremon"));
        commentModelList.add(new CommentModel("","Ooo where did you get this...","","1 aug","","","pako"));

        commentAdapter = new CommentAdapter(CommentActivity.this,commentModelList);

        LinearLayoutManager linearLayoutManager = new LinearLayoutManager(CommentActivity.this);
        linearLayoutManager.setOrientation(RecyclerView.VERTICAL);
        recyclerView.setAdapter(commentAdapter);
        recyclerView.setLayoutManager(linearLayoutManager);
        commentAdapter.notifyDataSetChanged();






    }

03/05/23, 8:09â€¯am - Rishabh: import tkinter as tk
from tkinter import *
from tkinter import messagebox
from tkinter import messagebox
def show_message(title,message):
    messagebox.showerror(title,message)
    
# Create a Tkinter window
window = Tk()
window.title("Gaurav Budget app Login")
window.geometry("400x400")

username_label = Label(window, text="username:")
username_label.pack()
username_entry = Entry(window)
username_entry.pack()

password_label = Label(window, text="password:")
password_label.pack()
password_entry = Entry(window, show="*")
password_entry.pack()

def login():
    username = username_entry.get()
    password = password_entry.get()
    if username == "Gaurav" and password == "12345":
        print("Login successful!")
    else:
        show_message("Error",'Incorrect Password')
        return
def login():
    username = username_entry.get()
    password = password_entry.get()
    if username == "Gaurav" and password =="12345":
        print("Login successful!")
    else:
        show_message("Error",'Incorrect username')
        return
# Create login button and attach login function to it
login_button = Button(window, text="Login", command=login)
login_button.pack()

# Start the Tkinter event loop
window.mainloop()

class MainWindow:
    def __init__(self):
        self.root = tk.Tk() 
        self.root.geometry("900x900") 
        self.root.resizable(width=False, height=False)
        self.root.title("Budget Tool") 
        self.style = ('Monospace', 18)
        self.draw('Gaurav Budget App!')
        self.buttons()
        self.root.mainloop() 


    def draw(self, msg):
        self.frameText = tk.Frame(self.root, height=19, width=50)
        self.textBox = tk.Text(self.frameText, height=19, width=50, relief='flat', bg='light yellow', font=self.style)
        self.textBox.insert(1.0, msg)
        self.textBox.config(state='disabled')
        self.frameText.grid(row=0, column=0)
        self.textBox.pack(padx=3, pady=3)

    def buttons(self):
        self.frame = tk.Frame(self.root, height=1, width=50)
        self.frame.grid(row=0, column=1)
        self.label = tk.Label(self.frame, text='Your Budget:')
        self.entry = tk.Entry(self.frame, font=12)
       # self.calBudget = tk.Button(self.frame, text='Calculate Budget', command=self.calculateBudget, width=20)
        self.viewBudget = tk.Button(self.frame, text='View Budget Plan', command=self.viewBudgetPlan, width=20)
        self.viewSpending = tk.Button(self.frame, text='View Spending Budget', command=self.popUp, width=20)
        items = [self.label, self.entry, self.viewBudget, self.viewSpending]
        for item in items: item.pack(padx=10, pady=20)

    def popUp(self):
        self.popUp = tk.Tk()
        self.popUp.geometry("400x400")
        self.popUp.title("Rent & Bills")
        self.popUp.resizable(width=False, height=False)
        self.rentLabel = tk.Label(self.popUp, text="Rent:")
        self.rentEntry = tk.Entry(self.popUp, width=25)
        self.GroceryLabel = tk.Label(self.popUp, text="Grocery:")
        self.GroceryEntry = tk.Entry(self.popUp, width=25)
        self.MedicalLabel = tk.Label(self.popUp, text="Medical Bills:")
        self.MedicalEntry = tk.Entry(self.popUp, width=25)
        self.MMLabel = tk.Label(self.popUp, text="Micelleneous Expense:")
        self.MMEntry = tk.Entry(self.popUp, width=25)
        self.done = tk.Button(self.popUp, text='Done', command=self.calculateSpending)
        items = [self.rentLabel, self.rentEntry,  self.GroceryLabel, self.GroceryEntry, self.MedicalLabel, self.MedicalEntry, self.MMLabel, self.MMEntry, self.done]
        for item in items: item.pack(pady=5)

#   FUNCTIONS   #


    def calculateBudget(self):
        self.budget = float(self.entry.get() or 0)
        
        self.spending = self.budget * 0.5
        self.draw(f"Total Budget: ${'{:.2f}'.format(self.budget)}\nSpending Money: ${'{:.2f}'.format(self.spending)}")
    
    def viewBudgetPlan(self):
        self.budget = float(self.entry.get() or 0)
        self.spending = self.budget * 0.5
        self.savings = self.budget - self.spending
        self.extra = self.budget - self.spending - self.savings
        self.draw(f"Total Budget\t\t: {'{:.2f}'.format(self.budget)}Rs\nSpending Money\t\t: {'{:.2f}'.format(self.spending)}Rs \
            \nTo Save\t\t: {'{:.2f}'.format(self.savings)}Rs")

    def calculateSpending(self):
        self.rent = float(self.rentEntry.get() or 0)
        self.Grocery = float(self.GroceryEntry.get() or 0)
        self.Medical = float(self.MedicalEntry.get() or 0)
        self.MM = float(self.MMEntry.get() or 0)
        self.popUp.destroy()
        self.budget = float(self.entry.get() or 0)
        self.food = (self.budget) - self.rent - self.Grocery - self.Medical - self.MM
        self.food2=self.rent + self.Grocery + self.Medical +self.MM
        self.draw(f"### TOTAL BUDGET ###\nTotal\t\t: {'{:.2f}'.format(self.budget)}Rs\nRemainig Money\t\t: {'{:.2f}'.format(self.food)}Rs\nSpending Money\t\t: {'{:.2f}'.format(self.food2)}Rs \
            \n\n### EXPENSES ###\nRent\t\t: {'{:.2f}'.format(self.rent)}Rs\nGrocery\t\t: {'{:.2f}'.format(self.Grocery)}Rs\nMecial\t\t: {'{:.2f}'.format(self.Medical)}Rs\nMiscellenous\t\t: {'{:.2f}'.format(self.MM)}Rs")

if __name__ == '__main__':
    MainWindow()
03/05/23, 8:09â€¯am - Rishabh: class Authentication(object):
    def __init__(self, username = ''):
        self.username = username

    def __lower(self):
        lower = any(c.islower() for c in self.username)
        return lower

    def __upper(self):
        upper = any(c.isupper() for c in self.username)
        return upper

    def __digit(self):
        digit = any(c.isdigit() for c in  self.username)
        return digit

    def validate(self):
        lower = self.__lower()
        upper = self.__upper()
        digit = self.__digit()

        length = len(self.username)

        report =  lower and upper and digit and length >= 6

        if report:
            print("Username passed all checks ")
            return True

        elif not lower:
            print("You didnt use Lower case letter")
            return False

        elif not upper:
            print("You didnt userUpper case letter")
            return False

        elif length <6:
            print("username should Atleast have 6 character")
            return False

        elif not digit:
            print("You didnt use Digit")
            return False
        else:
            pass

C = Authentication("ga1Agdfd")
print(C.validate())

05/05/23, 9:29â€¯am - Beluga2.0: POS tagging (part-of-speech tagging) is the process of assigning grammatical parts of speech to words in a text corpus. This is typically done by using computational algorithms and machine learning models to analyze the words in a sentence or text and determine the appropriate part of speech for each word, such as noun, verb, adjective, or adverb.
05/05/23, 9:30â€¯am - Beluga2.0: POS tagging has various applications in natural language processing, including:

Machine Translation: POS tagging can help improve the accuracy of machine translation systems by allowing for better understanding of the grammatical structure of the source text.

Named Entity Recognition: POS tagging can be used to identify proper nouns and other named entities in text, which is useful in information extraction applications such as identifying people, organizations, and locations.

Sentiment Analysis: POS tagging can be used to identify adjectives and adverbs in text, which can help determine the sentiment or tone of the text.

Text-to-Speech Conversion: POS tagging can be used to generate more natural-sounding speech by helping to identify the appropriate pronunciation and intonation for each word.

Information Retrieval: POS tagging can be used to improve the accuracy of search results by allowing for more sophisticated query processing, such as searching for specific parts of speech or combinations of parts of speech.
05/05/23, 9:50â€¯am - Rishabh: Nora
05/05/23, 10:13â€¯am - Beluga2.0: HMM stands for Hidden Markov Model used for sequence modeling and analysis.
It is based on two key concepts: Hidden States and Markov Process.
Hidden States are not directly observable but can be inferred from observed data, representing linguistic features.
Markov Process is a stochastic process where future state depends only on the current state.
HMM models a sequence of observations as a sequence of hidden states generating them.
It consists of two main components: Transition Probabilities and Emission Probabilities.
Transition Probabilities define the probability of transitioning from one hidden state to another.
Emission Probabilities define the probability of observing a particular output given a hidden state.
HMMs can compute the probability of a sequence of observations or generate new sequences.
HMMs are widely used in NLP for speech recognition, POS tagging, machine translation, bioinformatics, and finance.

  const searchParams = useSearchParams()
 
  const search = searchParams.get('search')
 
  // URL -> `/dashboard?search=my-project`
  // `search` -> 'my-project'
  return <>Search: {search}</>
}
